\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacehalf__float_1_1detail_a2d6a65bc1f34f19797f558a31deefe84}\label{namespacehalf__float_1_1detail_a2d6a65bc1f34f19797f558a31deefe84}} 
\index{half\_float::detail@{half\_float::detail}!half\_cast@{half\_cast}}
\index{half\_cast@{half\_cast}!half\_float::detail@{half\_float::detail}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{half\_cast()}{half\_cast()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename T , typename U $>$ \\
T half\+\_\+float\+::detail\+::half\+\_\+cast (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{U}]{arg }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Cast to or from half-\/precision floating point number. This casts between \mbox{\hyperlink{classhalf__float_1_1half}{half}} and any built-\/in arithmetic type. The values are converted directly using the given rounding mode, without any roundtrip over {\ttfamily float} that a {\ttfamily static\+\_\+cast} would otherwise do. It uses the default rounding mode.

Using this cast with neither of the two types being a \mbox{\hyperlink{classhalf__float_1_1half}{half}} or with any of the two types not being a built-\/in arithmetic type (apart from \mbox{\hyperlink{classhalf__float_1_1half}{half}}, of course) results in a compiler error and casting between \mbox{\hyperlink{classhalf__float_1_1half}{half}}s is just a no-\/op. 
\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em T} & destination type (half or built-\/in arithmetic type) \\
\hline
{\em U} & source type (half or built-\/in arithmetic type) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em arg} & value to cast \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\itshape arg} converted to destination type 
\end{DoxyReturn}

T half\+\_\+float\+::detail\+::half\+\_\+cast (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{U}]{arg }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Cast to or from half-\/precision floating point number. This casts between \mbox{\hyperlink{classhalf__float_1_1half}{half}} and any built-\/in arithmetic type. The values are converted directly using the given rounding mode, without any roundtrip over {\ttfamily float} that a {\ttfamily static\+\_\+cast} would otherwise do.

Using this cast with neither of the two types being a \mbox{\hyperlink{classhalf__float_1_1half}{half}} or with any of the two types not being a built-\/in arithmetic type (apart from \mbox{\hyperlink{classhalf__float_1_1half}{half}}, of course) results in a compiler error and casting between \mbox{\hyperlink{classhalf__float_1_1half}{half}}s is just a no-\/op.
